<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: center;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Faa Morena</span>&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">fala sobre os ingredientes que d&atilde;o um tempero especial ao Ritmo Brasil. Clique na imagem e veja o v&iacute;deo.</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: center;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; text-align: start;"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; text-align: start;">RITMO BRASIL &ndash; MUITA M&Uacute;SICA EM SUA VIDA!</span><br style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: normal; text-align: start;" /></span></p>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: justify;"></div>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: justify;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">&nbsp;</span></div>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: normal; text-align: start;">Todos os s&aacute;bados, &agrave;s 18h30, o Brasil tem um encontro marcado com a sua arte e cultura. &Eacute; o Ritmo Brasil, que pela RedeTV!, representa o principal espa&ccedil;o da m&uacute;sica brasileira na televis&atilde;o. Artistas consagrados e novos nomes do cen&aacute;rio musical nacional s&atilde;o os convidados da apresentadora Faa Morena que esbanja simpatia, irrever&ecirc;ncia e espontaneidade na condu&ccedil;&atilde;o do programa. Faa e seus convidados fazem do in&iacute;cio da noite de s&aacute;bado uma grande divers&atilde;o.&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;"></div>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;">Em todas as edi&ccedil;&otilde;es do programa, voc&ecirc; confere um papo descontra&iacute;do em que os artistas revelam detalhes de sua rela&ccedil;&atilde;o com fam&iacute;lia, amigos e f&atilde;s. Tudo regado ao som dos mais diferentes estilos musicais sem preconceitos. Al&eacute;m da MPB, h&aacute; espa&ccedil;o para o samba e o reggae, passando pelo sertanejo e pelo pop, sem deixar de lado, o cl&aacute;ssico e o rock. Tudo &eacute; sempre bem-vindo no Ritmo Brasil.&nbsp;</div>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;"></div>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333; text-align: center;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"></span></p>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;">Grandes nomes da m&uacute;sica nacional s&atilde;o a atra&ccedil;&atilde;o constante no programa que j&aacute; contou com a presen&ccedil;a de artistas como Ivete Sangalo, Claudia Leitte, Durval Lelys, Charlie Brown Jr., NXZero, Cine, Tihuana, CPM22, Detonautas, Pitty, Mutantes, Cidade Negra, Fresno, Maskavo, Onze:20, Falamansa, Jeito Moleque, Oba Oba Samba House, Inimigos da HP, Samb&ocirc;, S&eacute;rgio Reis, C&eacute;sar Menotti e Fabiano, Daniel, Fernando e Sorocaba, Eduardo Costa, Victor e Leo, Leonardo, Guilherme e Santiago, Maria Cec&iacute;lia e Rodolfo, Gusttavo Lima, Bruno e Marrone, Luan Santana, Roberta Miranda, Gian e Giovani, Edson e Hudson, Em&iacute;lio Santiago, MPB4, Roupa Nova, Z&eacute;lia Duncan, Claudio Zoli, Fernanda Porto, Maur&iacute;cio Manieri, Leo Maia, DJ Hum, MC Guim&ecirc;, MC Lon, MC Rodolfinho, Lenine, Frejat, Exaltasamba, Dudu Nobre, Fundo de Quintal, Olodum, Jair Rodrigues, Jorge Arag&atilde;o, Katinguel&ecirc;, Eliana de Lima, Osvaldinho da Cu&iacute;ca, Quinteto em Branco e Preto, Leci Brand&atilde;o, Elba Ramalho, Amado Batista, Maite Perroni, Dulce Mar&iacute;a e Christian Chavez, entre muitos outros.</div>
